## Biologist calls for protection and more studies of natural time capsules of climate change
 - [https://phys.org/news/2024-05-biologist-natural-capsules-climate.html](https://phys.org/news/2024-05-biologist-natural-capsules-climate.html)
 - RSS feed: 
 - date published: 2024-05-30T20:42:47.855841+00:00

Packrats, also known as woodrats, are the original hoarders, collecting materials from their environment to make their nests, called middens. In deserts throughout western North America, for instance, packrat middens can preserve plants, insects, bones and other specimens for more than 50,000 years, offering scientists a snapshot into the past.

## Reduced sulfur content in shipping fuel associated with increased maritime atmospheric warming
 - [https://phys.org/news/2024-05-sulfur-content-shipping-fuel-maritime.html](https://phys.org/news/2024-05-sulfur-content-shipping-fuel-maritime.html)
 - RSS feed: 
 - date published: 2024-05-30T15:32:48.607546+00:00

An 80% reduction in sulfur dioxide shipping emissions observed in early 2020 could be associated with substantial atmospheric warming over some ocean regions, according to a modeling study published in Communications Earth &amp; Environment. The sudden decline in emissions was a result of the introduction of the International Maritime Organization's 2020 regulation (IMO 2020), which reduced the maximum sulfur content allowed in shipping fuel from 3.5% to 0.5% to help reduce air pollution.
